style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;font-weight:bold;">DR PEPPER SNAPPLE GROUP REPORTS </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;color:#000000;font-weight:bold;text-decoration:none;">FOURTH</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;font-weight:bold;">&#32;QUARTER AND FULL YEAR </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;color:#000000;font-weight:bold;text-decoration:none;">2013</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;font-weight:bold;">&#32;RESULTS</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-top:12px;text-align:center;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:13px;text-align:center;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Reported EPS were $.78 for the quarter. Reported EPS were $3.05 for the year, up 3%.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:13px;text-align:center;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Core EPS were $.97 for the quarter. Core EPS were $3.20 for the year, up 10%.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:13px;text-align:center;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Net sales decreased 1% for the quarter and were flat for the full year.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:13px;text-align:center;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Year-to-date, the company returned $702 million to shareholders. </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">Plano, TX, Feb. 12, 2014 - Dr Pepper Snapple Group, Inc. (NYSE: DPS) reported fourth quarter 2013 EPS of $0.78 compared to $0.81 in the prior year period. Core EPS were $0.97, up 18.3% compared to $0.82 in the prior year. </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">For the quarter, reported net sales decreased 1%. Sales volume declines of 4% and less favorable trade adjustments were partially offset by favorable mix and price. Reported segment operating profit (SOP) decreased 7%, or $27 million, as a $56 million non-cash charge due to our intention to withdraw from a multi-employer pension plan and the volume decline were partially offset by a year-over-year LIFO benefit of $25 million and favorable price and mix. Reported income from operations for the quarter was $264 million, including $3 million of unrealized commodity mark-to-market losses. Reported income from operations was $292 million in the prior year period, including $1 million of unrealized commodity mark-to-market losses. Core income from operations was $323 million, up 10.2% compared to the prior year period.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">For the year, reported net sales were flat. Reported income from operations was $1,046 million, compared to $1,092 million in the prior year period. Core income from operations was $1,123 million, up 3.7% compared to the prior year period. For the year, the company reported earnings of $3.05 per diluted share compared to $2.96 per diluted share in the prior year period.  Excluding a $16 million unrealized commodity mark-to-market loss in the current year and a $17 million unrealized commodity mark-to-market gain in the prior year period, and certain items affecting comparability in both years, Core EPS were $3.20 compared to $2.92 in the prior year period.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">DPS President and CEO Larry Young said, &#8220;I am proud of the team&#8217;s ability to remain focused and execute against our strategy during a challenging year. We continued to gain distribution and availability across our key brands and packages and grew volume share and held dollar share in the highly competitive CSD category.&#8221; </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;"><br></font></div><br><div style="text-align:center;"><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">1</font></div></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"><a name="s98DA318B4F7CDDDA6E53EBF59D612466"></a><div></div><br><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">Young continued, &#8220;Our Core 4 and RC TEN platform is bringing lapsed consumer occasions back to the CSD category, and Rapid Continuous Improvement (RCI) continues to provide meaningful improvements while strengthening organizational capabilities. As we move into 2014, our teams will continue to build the TEN platform with programming focused on driving awareness and trial, provide consumers with balanced beverage options and execute with excellence in the marketplace.&#8221;    </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-top:12px;text-align:left;font-size:12pt;"><div style="padding-left:0px;text-indent:0px;line-height:normal;padding-top:10px;"><table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-family:Times New style="font-family:inherit;font-size:8pt;">BCS - bottler case sales</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;font-weight:bold;">BCS Volume </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">For the quarter, BCS volume declined 2% with both carbonated soft drinks (CSDs) and non-carbonated beverages (NCBs) declining 2%.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><br><div style="text-align:center;"><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">2</font></div></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"><a name="s98DA318B4F7CDDDA6E53EBF59D612466"></a><div></div><br><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">In CSDs, the category continued to face significant headwinds. Dr Pepper volume decreased 1%. Our Core 4 brands, which include TEN, declined 4% as a high-single digit decrease in 7UP and mid-single digit declines in Sunkist soda and A&amp;W were partially offset by a mid-single digit increase in Canada Dry. Squirt and RC Cola both declined mid-single digits. Sun Drop declined double-digits while Pe&#241;afiel increased double-digits. Fountain foodservice volume increased 2% in the quarter.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">In NCBs, Hawaiian Punch volume declined 8%. This decline was partially offset by a 3% increase in Snapple. Mott&#8217;s was flat in the quarter. </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">By geography, U.S. and Canada volume declined 2%, and Mexico and the Caribbean volume increased 4%.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">For the year, BCS volume decreased 2% with both carbonated soft drinks (CSDs) and non-carbonated beverages (NCBs) declining 2%. </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">Dr Pepper volume decreased 2% and our Core 4 brands, which include TEN, declined 1% as mid-single digit declines in 7UP and Sunkist soda and a low-single digit decrease in A&amp;W were partially offset by a mid-single digit increase in Canada Dry. Crush, Squirt and RC Cola all declined mid-single digits while Sun Drop declined double-digits. Pe&#241;afiel increased double-digits and Schweppes increased mid-single digits. Fountain foodservice volume was flat for the year.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">In NCBs, Hawaiian Punch volume declined 9%. This decline was partially offset by a 2% increase in Snapple and a mid-single digit increase in Mott&#8217;s.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">By geography, U.S. and Canada volume declined 2%, and Mexico and the Caribbean volume increased 3%.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><br><div style="text-align:center;"><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">3</font></div></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"><a name="s98DA318B4F7CDDDA6E53EBF59D612466"></a><div></div><br><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;font-weight:bold;">Beverage Concentrates</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">Net sales for the quarter decreased 3% as concentrate price increases taken earlier in the year and favorable mix were more than offset by a 6% volume decline and less favorable trade adjustments. SOP decreased 1% as the net sales decline was partially offset by lower marketing investments of $8 million. </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;font-weight:bold;">Packaged Beverages</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">Net sales declined 2% for the quarter on a 2% volume decline, which was partially offset by favorable product and package mix. SOP decreased 18% as a $56 million non-cash charge due to our intention to withdraw from a multi-employer pension plan and the volume decline were partially offset by a year-over-year LIFO benefit of $24 million, lower people costs and favorable pricing.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;font-weight:bold;">Latin America Beverages</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">Net sales for the quarter increased 9% reflecting favorable mix and a 4% increase in sales volumes. SOP increased 14% as net sales growth and ongoing productivity improvements were partially offset by increases in people costs, commodity cost increases, higher marketing investments and increases in transportation and other manufacturing costs.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;font-weight:bold;">Corporate and other items</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">For the quarter, corporate costs totaled $73 million, including a $3 million unrealized commodity mark-to-market loss. Corporate costs in the prior year period were $73 million, including a $1 million unrealized commodity mark-to-market loss. </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">For the year, corporate costs totaled $309 million, including $16 million of unrealized commodity mark-to-market losses. Corporate costs in the prior year period were $261 million, including a $17 million unrealized commodity mark-to-market gain. </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">Net interest expense decreased $2 million for the quarter compared to the prior year.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">For the quarter, the effective tax rate was 34.2%. For the year, the reported effective tax rate was a negative 14.9%, as the completion of an IRS audit decreased our effective tax rate by 50.4%. The effective tax rate in the prior year period was 35.7%.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;font-weight:bold;">Cash flow</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">For the year, the company generated $866 million of cash from operating activities compared to $482 million in the prior year period. The prior year period included tax payments of $531 million related to the PepsiCo and Coca-Cola licensing agreements. Capital spending totaled $179 million compared to $217 million in the prior year period. The company returned $702 million to shareholders in the form of stock repurchases ($400 million) and dividends ($302 million).</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;"><br></font></div><br><div style="text-align:center;"><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">4</font></div></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"><a name="s98DA318B4F7CDDDA6E53EBF59D612466"></a><div></div><br><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;font-weight:bold;">2014 full year guidance</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">The company expects full year reported net sales to be flat to up 1% and Core EPS to be in the $3.38 to $3.46 range.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">Packaging and ingredient costs are expected to decrease COGS by 2%, on a constant volume/mix basis. </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">The company expects its core tax rate to be approximately 35.5%.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">The company expects capital spending to be approximately 3% of net sales.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">The company expects to repurchase $375 million to $400 million of its common stock.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;font-weight:bold;">Definitions</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">Bottler case sales (BCS) volume: Sales of finished beverages, in equivalent 288 fluid ounce cases, sold by the company and its bottling partners to retailers and independent distributors and excludes contract manufacturing volume. Volume for products sold by the company and its bottling partners is reported on a monthly basis, with the fourth quarter comprising October, November and December.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">Sales volume: Sales of concentrates and finished beverages, in equivalent 288 fluid ounce cases, shipped by the company to its bottlers, retailers and independent distributors and includes contract manufacturing volume.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">Pricing refers to the impact of list price changes.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">Unrealized mark-to-market: We recognize the change in the fair value of open commodity derivative positions between periods in corporate unallocated expenses, as these instruments do not qualify for hedge accounting treatment. As the underlying commodity is delivered, the realized gains and losses are subsequently reflected in the segment results. </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">EPS represents diluted earnings per share.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">Core tax rate is defined as the effective tax rate on core earnings. </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">Core income from operations is defined as income from operations adjusted for the unrealized mark-to-market impact of commodity derivatives and certain items that are excluded for comparison to prior year periods.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">Core operating margin is defined as the core income from operations divided by core net sales.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">Core Earnings is defined as earnings adjusted for the unrealized mark-to-market impact of commodity derivatives and certain items that are excluded for comparison to prior year periods.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">Core EPS represents Core Earnings per share.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:12pt;"><font Our success is fueled by more than 50 brands that are synonymous with refreshment, fun and flavor. We have 6 of the top 10 non-cola soft drinks, and 13 of our 14 leading brands are No. 1 or No. 2 in their flavor categories. In addition to our flagship Dr Pepper and Snapple brands, our portfolio includes 7UP, A&amp;W, Canada Dry, Clamato, Crush, Hawaiian Punch, Mott's, Mr &amp; Mrs T mixers, Pe&#241;afiel, Rose's, Schweppes, Squirt and Sunkist soda. To learn more about our iconic brands and Plano, Texas-based company, please visit www.DrPepperSnapple.com. The certain item excluded for the </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;color:#000000;text-decoration:none;">twelve months ended</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">&#32;</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;color:#000000;font-weight:normal;text-decoration:none;">December&#160;31, 2013</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">&#32;and </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;color:#000000;font-weight:normal;text-decoration:none;">2012</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">, relates to the tax payments resulting from the licensing agreements with PepsiCo and Coca-Cola.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-top:12px;text-align:justify;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;font-weight:bold;">Core Earnings: </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">Core Earnings is defined as Reported Earnings adjusted for the unrealized mark-to-market impact of commodity derivatives and certain items that are excluded for comparison to prior year periods. The certain items excluded for the three and </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;color:#000000;text-decoration:none;">twelve months ended</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">&#32;</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;color:#000000;font-weight:normal;text-decoration:none;">December&#160;31, 2013</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">&#32;are (i) separation-related charges, primarily the completion of the IRS audit, a separation-related foreign deferred tax charge and the associated impacts under the Tax Indemnity Agreement with Mondel&#275;z, (ii) an adjustment to a previously disclosed legal provision, (iii) restructuring charges and (iv) a non-cash charge related to our intention to withdraw from a multi-employer pension plan. capital lease executed prior to the separation from Cadbury.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-top:12px;text-align:justify;font-size:10pt;"><font
